					<h2 id="mainHeading">Site Help</h2>
					
					<p>This section of the web site was created to help you find what you're looking for if you're having trouble. The site has been completely redesigned with ease-of-use as a top priority but occasionally some things can be overlooked.</p>

					<p>Please select from the following options:</p>
					
					<dl>
						<dt><a href="/Help/BugReport.asp" rel="nofollow">Report a Bug</a></dt>
						<dd>Found a bug or error on the site? Say it isn't so! Yes, we're human too and make mistakes &hellip; let us know what's wrong and we'll be right on it!</dd>
						
						<dt><a href="/Help/Privacy.asp">Privacy Policy</a></dt>
						<dd>Read this to find out what we do and don't do with any information collected by this site.</dd>
						
						<dt><a href="/Help/Copyright.asp">Trademarks and Copyrights</a></dt>
						<dd>This page lists our various copyrights, trademarks and other legal information.</dd>
